|CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER PSUCURRENCY_CD_TBL BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE  ON PS_CURRENCY_CD_TBL FOR EACH ROW DECLARE PSSYSID  NUMBER (31,0);|~ 
|PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;|~ 
|BEGIN|~ 
|IF INSERTING THEN|~ 
|SELECT MAX(SYNCID) INTO PSSYSID FROM PS_CURRENCY_CD_TBL WHERE  :NEW.CURRENCY_CD = PS_CURRENCY_CD_TBL.CURRENCY_CD;|~ 
|IF PSSYSID <= 0 OR PSSYSID IS NULL THEN|~ 
|UPDATE PSSYSTEMID SET PTNEXTSYSTEMID = PTNEXTSYSTEMID + 1 WHERE RECNAME = 'CURRENCY_CD_TBL';|~ 
|SELECT PTNEXTSYSTEMID INTO PSSYSID FROM PSSYSTEMID WHERE RECNAME='CURRENCY_CD_TBL';|~ 
|:NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|ELSE|~ 
|:NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|END IF;|~ 
|END IF;|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|COMMIT;|~ 
|END;|~ 
|/|~

|/|~ 
|CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER PSUPSMPRTPREF BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE  ON PSMPRTPREF FOR EACH ROW DECLARE PSSYSID  NUMBER (31,0);|~ 
|PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;|~ 
|BEGIN|~ 
|IF INSERTING THEN  IF :NEW.SYNCID > 0 THEN|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|ELSE|~ 
|UPDATE PSSYSTEMID SET PTNEXTSYSTEMID = PTNEXTSYSTEMID + 1 WHERE RECNAME = 'PSMPRTPREF';|~ 
|SELECT PTNEXTSYSTEMID INTO PSSYSID FROM PSSYSTEMID WHERE RECNAME='PSMPRTPREF';  :NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|END IF;  ELSE|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;  END IF;|~ 
|COMMIT;|~ 
|END;|~ 
|/|~ 
||~

|CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER PSUPSTIMEZONE BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE  ON PSTIMEZONE FOR EACH ROW DECLARE PSSYSID  NUMBER (31,0);|~ 
|PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;|~ 
|BEGIN|~ 
|IF INSERTING THEN  IF :NEW.SYNCID > 0 THEN|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|ELSE|~ 
|UPDATE PSSYSTEMID SET PTNEXTSYSTEMID = PTNEXTSYSTEMID + 1 WHERE RECNAME = 'PSTIMEZONE';|~ 
|SELECT PTNEXTSYSTEMID INTO PSSYSID FROM PSSYSTEMID WHERE RECNAME='PSTIMEZONE';  :NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|END IF;  ELSE|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;  END IF;|~ 
|COMMIT;|~ 
|END;|~ 
|/|~

|/|~ 
|CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER PSUPSWORKLIST BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE  ON PSWORKLIST FOR EACH ROW DECLARE PSSYSID  NUMBER (31,0);|~ 
|PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;|~ 
|BEGIN|~ 
|IF INSERTING THEN  IF :NEW.SYNCID > 0 THEN|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|ELSE|~ 
|UPDATE PSSYSTEMID SET PTNEXTSYSTEMID = PTNEXTSYSTEMID + 1 WHERE RECNAME = 'PSWORKLIST';|~ 
|SELECT PTNEXTSYSTEMID INTO PSSYSID FROM PSSYSTEMID WHERE RECNAME='PSWORKLIST';  :NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|END IF;  ELSE|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;  END IF;|~ 
|COMMIT;|~ 
|END;|~

|-- Start the Transaction|~ 
||~ 
||~ 
|-- Create temporary table|~ 
||~ 
|CREATE TABLE PSYPTGRANTTBL (GRANT_TYPE VARCHAR2(1) NOT NULL,   TABLENAME VARCHAR2(30) NOT NULL) SEGMENT CREATION DEFERRED   PCTFREE 10 PCTUSED 80 INITRANS 1 MAXTRANS 255 NOCOMPRESS LOGGING  STORAGE( INITIAL 40960 NEXT 106496 MAXEXTENTS 2147483645  PCTINCREASE 0)  TABLESPACE "PTTBL"|~ 
|/|~ 
||~ 
|-- Copy from source to temp table|~ 
||~ 
|INSERT INTO PSYPTGRANTTBL (        GRANT_TYPE,    TABLENAME)  SELECT        ' ',    TABLENAME  FROM PTGRANTTBL|~ 
|/|~ 
||~ 
|-- CAUTION: Drop Original Table|~ 
||~ 
|DROP TABLE PTGRANTTBL|~ 
|/|~ 
||~ 
|-- Rename Table|~ 
||~ 
|RENAME PSYPTGRANTTBL TO PTGRANTTBL|~ 
|/|~ 
||~ 
|-- Done|~ 
||~

|CREATE OR REPLACE TRIGGER PSURT_RATE_TBL BEFORE INSERT OR UPDATE  ON PS_RT_RATE_TBL FOR EACH ROW DECLARE PSSYSID  NUMBER (31,0);|~ 
|PRAGMA AUTONOMOUS_TRANSACTION;|~ 
|BEGIN|~ 
|IF INSERTING THEN|~ 
|SELECT MAX(SYNCID) INTO PSSYSID FROM PS_RT_RATE_TBL WHERE  :NEW.RT_RATE_INDEX = PS_RT_RATE_TBL.RT_RATE_INDEX  AND :NEW.TERM = PS_RT_RATE_TBL.TERM  AND :NEW.FROM_CUR = PS_RT_RATE_TBL.FROM_CUR  AND :NEW.TO_CUR = PS_RT_RATE_TBL.TO_CUR  AND :NEW.RT_TYPE = PS_RT_RATE_TBL.RT_TYPE;|~ 
|IF PSSYSID <= 0 OR PSSYSID IS NULL THEN|~ 
|UPDATE PSSYSTEMID SET PTNEXTSYSTEMID = PTNEXTSYSTEMID + 1 WHERE RECNAME = 'RT_RATE_TBL';|~ 
|SELECT PTNEXTSYSTEMID INTO PSSYSID FROM PSSYSTEMID WHERE RECNAME='RT_RATE_TBL';|~ 
|:NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|ELSE|~ 
|:NEW.SYNCID:= PSSYSID;|~ 
|END IF;|~ 
|END IF;|~ 
|:NEW.LASTUPDDTTM := SYSDATE;|~ 
|COMMIT;|~ 
|END;|~ 
|/|~
